[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring fuzzing tests. The crash occurs in the `alliswellprotocoll_sm` function at [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95malliswellprotocoll.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m253:33[0m[39m` when attempting to perform a WRITE [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory access to address [0m[1;36m0x000000000000[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe zero page[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This is a null-deref [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability with a SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, indicating high severity.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### What the Issue Is[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue manifests as an AddressSanitizer SEGV [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSegmentation Fault[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m error during [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe execution of the `curl_fuzzer_ws` fuzzer. The crash is triggered by a null [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointer dereference, specifically a WRITE memory access to the zero page [0m[1;39m([0m[39maddress [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0x000000000000[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The error occurs consistently when processing a specific test case[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput during fuzzing.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **null pointer dereference vulnerability** that leads to a segmentation [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfault. The vulnerability is classified with a SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m and labeled as [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"null-deref"[0m[39m by AddressSanitizer. The signal is caused by a WRITE memory access [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempt to a null pointer, which is a critical memory safety issue.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Important Observations and Findings[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Crash Location**: The primary crash occurs at line [0m[1;36m253[0m[39m, column [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m in [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95malliswellprotocoll.c[0m[39m` within the `alliswellprotocoll_sm` function.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Call Stack Analysis**: The vulnerability is triggered through the following [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcall chain:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzzer entry point: `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`[0m                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Final crash point: `alliswellprotocoll_sm`[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Fuzzing Context**: The crash occurs during fuzzing with:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzzing engine: libfuzzer[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m runs on a single test case[0m                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto a null pointer, suggesting that a pointer variable was not properly initialized [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor validated before use.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m76[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlib/alliswellprotocoll.[0m[1;92mc:150[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m169[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m150[0m[39m:static CURLcode [0m[1;35malliswellprotocoll_do[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstruct Curl_easy *data, bool *done[0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m151[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m152[0m[39m:  *done = FALSE; [0m[35m/[0m[39m* unconditionally *[0m[35m/[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m153[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m154[0m[39m:  return CURLE_OK;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m155[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m156[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m157[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m* The only way to change state *[0m[35m/[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m158[0m[39m:static void [0m[1;35mvnstate[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstruct Curl_easy *data,[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m159[0m[39m:                    enum alliswellprotocollstate state[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m160[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m161[0m[39m:  struct connectdata *conn = data->conn;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m162[0m[39m:  struct alliswellprotocoll_conn *vnormal = &conn->proto.vnormal;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m163[0m[39m:#ifdef DEBUGBUILD[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m164[0m[39m:  [0m[1;35minfof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, [0m[32m"%d [0m[32m([0m[32mfrom %d[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m165[0m[39m:        state,[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m166[0m[39m:        vnormal->state[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m167[0m[39m:#endif[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m168[0m[39m:  vnormal->state = state;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m169[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter thoroughly analyzing the code snippets and evaluation report, I have [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentified the root cause and nature of the vulnerability:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Issue: Null Pointer Dereference at Line [0m[1;36m253[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe crash occurs at `[0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95malliswellprotocoll.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m253:33[0m[39m` with this incorrect[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*[0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned int *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mresult = CURLE_OK;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Root Cause:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `result` is declared as `CURLcode result = CURLE_OK;` at line [0m[1;36m174[0m[39m, which is an [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menum/integer type [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvalue [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m for CURLE_OK[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The code incorrectly casts this integer value [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to a pointer: `[0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned int [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Then attempts to dereference and write to address [0m[1;36m0x0[0m[39m, causing a WRITE to the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mzero page[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This is a classic null pointer dereference vulnerability[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Evidence from Codebase:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAll other pingpong-based protocol state machines [0m[1;39m([0m[39mFTP, IMAP, POP3, SMTP[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsistently use the pattern `result = CURLE_OK;` without any pointer casting. The [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpingpong infrastructure expects the state machine callback to return a `CURLcode` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalue directly, as confirmed by the function signature at `lib/pingpong.h:[0m[1;36m70[0m[39m` and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe call at `lib/pingpong.[0m[1;92mc:137[0m[39m`.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Secondary Issue: Unchecked Memory Allocation[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAt lines [0m[1;36m116[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m118[0m[39m in `alliswellprotocoll_conn`, three `calloc` calls allocate memory[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout checking for NULL returns:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvnormal->state1 = [0m[1;35mcalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m128[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvnormal->state2 = [0m[1;35mcalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m128[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvnormal->state3 = [0m[1;35mcalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m128[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThese pointers are subsequently used at lines [0m[1;36m204[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m218[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m237[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39marray writes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m216[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m235[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m250[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmemcmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and [0m[1;36m206[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m221[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m240[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCurl_pp_sendf[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without validation. If any [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation fails, these operations will cause crashes.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Patch [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Fix Null Pointer Dereference [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPrimary Fix[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** `[0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95malliswellprotocoll.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m253[0m[39m`[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change:**[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace the incorrect pointer cast and dereference:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*[0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned int *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mresult = CURLE_OK;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith the correct assignment:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresult = CURLE_OK;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification:**[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This matches the pattern used by all other pingpong protocol implementations [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mFTP, IMAP, POP3, SMTP[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The pingpong state machine infrastructure expects a `CURLcode` return value, not [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointer manipulation[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This is clearly a typo or copy-paste error that should be a simple assignment[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Patch [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Add Memory Allocation Failure Checks [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSecondary Fix[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** `[0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95malliswellprotocoll.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m106[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m120[0m[39m`[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change:**[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter each `calloc` call in the `alliswellprotocoll_conn` function, add NULL checks[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand return `CURLE_OUT_OF_MEMORY` on failure:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstatic CURLcode [0m[1;35malliswellprotocoll_conn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstruct Curl_easy *data, bool *done[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  *done = FALSE;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  struct alliswellprotocoll_conn *vnormal = &[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata->conn->proto.vnormal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  struct pingpong *pp = &[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata->conn->proto.vnormal.pp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  struct connectdata *conn = data->conn;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;35mPINGPONG_SETUP[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpp, alliswellprotocoll_sm, vnormal_endofresp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;35mCurl_pp_init[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  vnormal->state1 = [0m[1;35mcalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m128[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39m!vnormal->state1[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return CURLE_OUT_OF_MEMORY;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  vnormal->state2 = [0m[1;35mcalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m128[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39m!vnormal->state2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvnormal->state1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return CURLE_OUT_OF_MEMORY;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39m!vnormal->state3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  return [0m[1;35mCurl_pp_statemach[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, pp, FALSE, FALSE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification:**[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This follows the standard curl pattern for handling memory allocation failures [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mas seen in FTP code at lines [0m[1;36m2936[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2937[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Prevents potential crashes when memory allocation fails[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Properly cleans up previously allocated memory on subsequent allocation failures[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Returns the standard `CURLE_OUT_OF_MEMORY` error code[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Strategy is Optimal[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Addresses Root Cause:** The primary fix directly resolves the reported null [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointer dereference by removing the incorrect pointer cast and dereference.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic:** The fix maintains the intended behavior of setting[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`result = CURLE_OK` in the success path of the DO3 state, just correcting the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation method.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Follows Established Patterns:** Both fixes align with patterns used throughout[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe curl codebase, particularly in other pingpong protocol implementations.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Minimal Impact:** The changes are surgical and localized, affecting only the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuggy code without touching the broader state machine logic, fuzzing [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minfrastructure, or protocol flow.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Defensive Programming:** The secondary fix adds robustness against memory [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation failures, preventing potential future crashes.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes:** The fixes maintain the same external API and behavior, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monly correcting internal implementation errors.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effects:**[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m expected. The primary fix corrects an obvious bug that prevents the code [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom working correctly.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The secondary fix only adds error handling that was missing, with no functional [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchange in the success path.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Testing Considerations:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer should no longer crash on the same input[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The protocol state machine should progress correctly through all states[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Memory allocation failure paths are now properly handled[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
